One option you should turn on right away is \"Add Hyperlinks to aid navigation\" found on the Options dialog. Finding your way around these three new reports will be difficult unless you do the following. Select any spreadsheet, but preferably the one called Sheet1. Double-clicking each entry under \"Changed Workbook Pairs\" will compare the workbooks for differences.\n\nWhy should you choose DiffEngineX when there are many other products around?
